function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }

	$tmp = pathinfo('includes/edition.ini');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/edition.ini')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/edition.ini', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/edition.ini');
}

if (!is_file('bcrypt_worker.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: bcrypt_worker.js');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('bcrypt_worker.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): bcrypt_worker.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('bcrypt_worker.js') != 'caf9b4fb4f5117afb7dd0e1d0f5d950e9848c942') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): bcrypt_worker.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('bcrypt_worker.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of bcrypt_worker.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('bcrypt_worker.js') !== 'caf9b4fb4f5117afb7dd0e1d0f5d950e9848c942') {
		if (@sha1_file('bcrypt_worker.js') !== 'e620fc99d1cf20dce2e0257f6636bf08898a55d9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: bcrypt_worker.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('bcrypt_worker.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('bcrypt_worker.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('bcrypt_worker.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('bcrypt_worker.js') !== 'caf9b4fb4f5117afb7dd0e1d0f5d950e9848c942') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): bcrypt_worker.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '79b1c9b840301ae6f14d6f49975b393d11f80a7d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '79b1c9b840301ae6f14d6f49975b393d11f80a7d') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'd8f643a6f008c65f211b82cacf006acf7658a9c5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '79b1c9b840301ae6f14d6f49975b393d11f80a7d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
